# 🏛️ COMPLETE 200-DAY CLAT 2026 PREPARATION ROADMAP
### From Absolute Zero to Exam-Ready | Covers All 5 Subjects | 3–4 Hours Daily

---

## 📌 ABOUT CLAT 2026
**CLAT** (Common Law Admission Test) is a national-level entrance exam for admission to undergraduate law programs (BA LLB / BBA LLB) at National Law Universities (NLUs) across India.

**Exam Expected:** December 2026  
**Duration:** 2 hours | **Questions:** 120 MCQs | **Marks:** 120 | **Negative Marking:** -0.25

### 5 Subjects:
1. **English Language** (22–26 questions) — Reading Comprehension, Vocabulary, Grammar
2. **Legal Reasoning** (35–39 questions) — Principles + Facts, Constitution, Torts, Contracts
3. **Logical Reasoning** (28–32 questions) — Critical Reasoning, Arguments, Syllogisms
4. **Current Affairs & GK** (13–17 questions) — News, Static GK, Legal Current Affairs
5. **Quantitative Techniques** (10–14 questions) — Basic Maths, Data Interpretation

---
## 📚 FREE RESOURCES MASTER LIST
- **English Grammar:** Wren & Martin (PDF free on Archive.org)
- **Legal:** NCERT Political Science Class 11 (Constitution at Work), Class 12
- **Maths:** NCERT Class 6–10 (ncert.nic.in — free download)
- **Current Affairs:** https://www.gktoday.in | https://www.affairscloud.com
- **Practice:** https://www.indiabix.com | https://www.clat.ac.in (past papers)
- **News Reading:** https://www.newsinlevels.com | The Hindu | Indian Express
- **YouTube — English:** "English Grammar by Spoken English Guru" channel
- **YouTube — Legal:** "LegalEdge CLAT" channel | "CLAT Possible" channel
- **YouTube — Logical:** "Unacademy CLAT" channel
- **YouTube — Maths:** "Khan Academy India" | "Arvind Academy" channel

---
## 🗓️ PHASE OVERVIEW
| Phase | Days | Focus |
|-------|------|-------|
| Phase 1: Foundation | 1–60 | Basics from scratch, slow & detailed |
| Phase 2: Practice | 61–150 | Medium difficulty, mixed questions |
| Phase 3: Mock Tests | 151–180 | Full-length mocks + analysis |
| Phase 4: Revision | 181–200 | Intensive revision + 2–3 mocks/week |

---

---
# 📘 PHASE 1: FOUNDATION (Days 1–60)
### Goal: Build basics in all 5 subjects from scratch. Slow, detailed, beginner-friendly.


---
## 📅 DAY 1
**Phase:** Foundation | **Daily Study:** 3–4 hours

**⏰ 4:00–4:45 | 📖 ENGLISH LANGUAGE**
- **Topic:** Parts of Speech — Nouns & Pronouns
- **Task:** Read the chapter explanation carefully (beginner — read twice if needed)
- **Source:** Wren & Martin Ch.1–2 | YouTube: 'Parts of Speech' by Spoken English Guru
- **Practice:** Attempt 10 grammar/comprehension questions on indiabix.com
- **Reading:** Read 1 editorial from newsinlevels.com (Level 2) — 5 mins
- **Vocabulary (10 words for today):** Abate, Aberrant, Abscond, Absolve, Abstain, Acrimony, Admonish, Adversity, Advocate, Affable
  → Write each word, its meaning, part of speech, and one example sentence in your notebook.

**⏰ 4:45–5:30 | ⚖️ LEGAL REASONING**
- **Topic:** What is Law? — Introduction, Legal System, Courts in India
- **Task:** Read the topic thoroughly. Make a 1-page handwritten summary.
- **Source:** YouTube: 'Introduction to Law' by LegalEdge CLAT
- **Practice:** Attempt 5 principle-fact questions (CLAT style) from clat.ac.in past papers or LegalEdge free material
- **Legal Current Affairs:** Read 1 legal news item from gktoday.in → Law & Constitution section

**⏰ 5:30–6:10 | 🧠 LOGICAL REASONING**
- **Topic:** Introduction to Arguments — Statements & Conclusions
- **Task:** Understand the concept with examples. Solve at least 2 examples yourself first.
- **Source:** YouTube: 'Logical Reasoning CLAT' by Unacademy CLAT
- **Practice:** Solve 8 questions on indiabix.com → Logical Reasoning (topic-wise)

**⏰ 6:10–6:45 | 🔢 QUANTITATIVE TECHNIQUES**
- **Topic:** Number System — Natural, Whole, Integers, BODMAS
- **Task:** Read NCERT chapter + watch 1 YouTube video (Arvind Academy or Khan Academy India)
- **Source:** NCERT Class 6 Ch.1–2 | Khan Academy India
- **Practice:** Solve 5–8 textbook/indiabix questions on today's topic

**⏰ 6:45–7:05 | 📰 CURRENT AFFAIRS & GK**
- **Task:** Read GKToday daily digest + 1 news article from The Hindu (Level 2 on newsinlevels.com)
- Visit gktoday.in → Daily Current Affairs and read today's digest (10–15 mins)
- Note 5 important facts in your GK diary

> **📝 End-of-Day Checklist:**
> ✅ Grammar/RC practice done | ✅ Legal summary written | ✅ LR questions solved | ✅ Maths practice done | ✅ 10 vocabulary words noted | ✅ GK diary updated

---
## 📅 DAY 7 — 🔁 WEEKLY REVISION DAY
### Theme: Revise Days 1–6 | Weekly Sectional Tests

**⏰ 4:00–4:40 PM | English Revision & Test**
- Revise all grammar topics from last 6 days (notes review)
- Practice: 15 grammar MCQs on indiabix.com → English Grammar
- Vocabulary review: Re-test yourself on last 60 words (Days 1–6)

**⏰ 4:40–5:20 PM | Legal Reasoning Revision & Test**
- Re-read all legal notes from the last 6 days
- Practice: 10 principle-fact sets from CLAT past papers or LegalEdge free tests
- Revise any 5 legal maxims covered this week

**⏰ 5:20–5:50 PM | Logical Reasoning Revision & Test**
- Quick re-read of LR concepts (statements, assumptions, etc.)
- Practice: 10 LR questions on indiabix.com → Logical Reasoning

**⏰ 5:50–6:20 PM | Quantitative Techniques Test**
- Practice: 10 maths questions from topics covered this week
- Source: indiabix.com → Arithmetic / NCERT exercises

**⏰ 6:20–7:00 PM | GK Weekly Revision**
- Write a 1-page summary of all current affairs from the last 7 days
- Go to affairscloud.com → Weekly GK Quiz and attempt 20 questions
- Review any 3 important news stories and note key facts

**📝 Vocabulary (10 words):** Deficient, Denounce, Depict, Derogatory, Deter, Dichotomy, Diligent, Discern, Discretion, Discriminate
> 📌 *Tip: On revision days, use a notebook to test yourself. Write answers before checking. This active recall boosts memory by 50%.*

- Revise any 5 legal maxims covered this week

**⏰ 5:20–5:50 PM | Logical Reasoning Revision & Test**
- Quick re-read of LR concepts (statements, assumptions, etc.)
- Practice: 10 LR questions on indiabix.com → Logical Reasoning

**⏰ 5:50–6:20 PM | Quantitative Techniques Test**
- Practice: 10 maths questions from topics covered this week
- Source: indiabix.com → Arithmetic / NCERT exercises

**⏰ 6:20–7:00 PM | GK Weekly Revision**
- Write a 1-page summary of all current affairs from the last 7 days

- Review any 3 important news stories and note key facts

**📝 Vocabulary (10 words):** Dissent, Doctrine, Dubious, Eminent, Empower, Equitable, Eradicate, Evade, Exonerate, Expedite
> 📌 *Tip: On revision days, use a notebook to test yourself. Write answers before checking. This active recall boosts memory by 50%.*

## 📅 DAY 42 — 🔁 WEEKLY REVISION DAY
### Theme: Revise Days 36–41 | Weekly Sectional Tests

**⏰ 4:00–4:40 PM | English Revision & Test**
- Revise all grammar topics from last 6 days (notes review)
- Practice: 15 grammar MCQs on indiabix.com → English Grammar
- Vocabulary review: Re-test yourself on last 60 words (Days 36–41)

**⏰ 4:40–5:20 PM | Legal Reasoning Revision & Test**
- Re-read all legal notes from the last 6 days
- Practice: 10 principle-fact sets from CLAT past papers or LegalEdge free tests
- Revise any 5 legal maxims covered this week

**⏰ 5:20–5:50 PM | Logical Reasoning Revision & Test**
- Quick re-read of LR concepts (statements, assumptions, etc.)
- Practice: 10 LR questions on indiabix.com → Logical Reasoning

**⏰ 5:50–6:20 PM | Quantitative Techniques Test**
- Practice: 10 maths questions from topics covered this week
- Source: indiabix.com → Arithmetic / NCERT exercises

**⏰ 6:20–7:00 PM | GK Weekly Revision**
- Write a 1-page summary of all current affairs from the last 7 days
- Go to affairscloud.com → Weekly GK Quiz and attempt 20 questions
- Review any 3 important news stories and note key facts

**📝 Vocabulary (10 words):** Aggravate, Allegation, Alleviate, Ambiguous, Amend, Amenable, Anarchy, Annul, Antiquated, Appease
> 📌 *Tip: On revision days, use a notebook to test yourself. Write answers before checking. This active recall boosts memory by 50%.*

- **Practice:** Solve 5–8 textbook/indiabix questions on today's topic

**⏰ 6:45–7:05 | 📰 CURRENT AFFAIRS & GK**
- **Task:** Static GK: Indian Polity, Geography, History brief notes + daily current affairs
- Visit gktoday.in → Daily Current Affairs and read today's digest (10–15 mins)
- Note 5 important facts in your GK diary

> **📝 End-of-Day Checklist:**
> ✅ Grammar/RC practice done | ✅ Legal summary written | ✅ LR questions solved | ✅ Maths practice done | ✅ 10 vocabulary words noted | ✅ GK diary updated

## 📅 DAY 61

- **Source:** Wren & Martin Ch.20
- **Vocabulary (10 words):** Abate, Aberrant, Abscond, Absolve, Abstain, Acrimony, Admonish, Adversity, Advocate, Affable

**⏰ 4:50–5:40 PM | ⚖️ LEGAL REASONING**
- **Topic:** Amendment Procedure & Basic Structure Doctrine
- **Practice:** Solve 2 principle-fact passage sets (10 questions total)
- **Focus:** Read the principle carefully. Apply ONLY the given principle to the given facts.
- **Source:** NCERT Class 11 Ch.9
- **Legal Current Affairs:** 1 legal news item from gktoday.in

**⏰ 5:40–6:20 PM | 🧠 LOGICAL REASONING**
- **Topic:** Critical Reasoning — Short Passages
- **Practice:** 1 full LR passage (5–6 questions, time: under 9 mins)
- **Also:** 5 standalone critical reasoning questions
- **Source:** CLAT sample papers

**⏰ 6:20–6:55 PM | 🔢 QUANTITATIVE TECHNIQUES**
- **Topic:** Compound Interest
- **Practice:** 8–10 questions (mix of today's topic + revision of previous topics)
- **DI Focus:** 1 small data interpretation table/graph (start from Day 95)
- **Source:** NCERT Class 8 Ch.8

**⏰ 6:55–7:15 PM | 📰 CURRENT AFFAIRS & GK**
- Read gktoday.in Daily Current Affairs digest
- Note: 3 National news, 2 International, 1 Legal/Judicial news
- Update your GK diary

> **📌 Phase 2 Strategy:** Start timing yourself. Set a stopwatch for each section. CLAT gives ~1 min per question. Build that instinct now.

- Time yourself: should complete in under 8 minutes

- Solve 10 mixed maths questions from all topics covered so far
- Source: indiabix.com → Mixed Arithmetic

- Attempt affairscloud.com → Weekly Quiz (20 questions)
- Review 5 important legal/polity GK facts

**📝 Vocabulary:** Claimant, Complainant, Contempt, Contract, Conveyance, Covenant, Damages, Defendant, Deposition, Discretionary

## 📅 DAY 133 — 🔁 WEEKLY REVISION DAY
### Theme: Revise Days 127–132 | Sectional Tests (Higher Level)

**⏰ 4:00–4:45 PM | English Sectional Test**
- Attempt 20 mixed English questions (RC + Grammar + Vocab) — indiabix.com or CLAT sample paper
- Review all wrong answers. Note the grammar rule violated.
- Vocabulary: Re-test 60 words from the last 6 days

**⏰ 4:45–5:30 PM | Legal Reasoning Sectional Test**
- Solve 2 full CLAT-style Legal Reasoning passage sets (principle + 4–5 questions each)
- Source: CLAT past papers (clat.ac.in) or LegalEdge CLAT free tests
- Revise 10 legal maxims from your notes

**⏰ 5:30–6:00 PM | Logical Reasoning Test**
- Solve 1 full LR passage set (5–6 questions)
- Time yourself: should complete in under 8 minutes
- Source: CLAT 2021–2023 official papers

**⏰ 6:00–6:30 PM | Quantitative Techniques Test**
- Solve 10 mixed maths questions from all topics covered so far
- Source: indiabix.com → Mixed Arithmetic

**⏰ 6:30–7:00 PM | GK Weekly Revision**
- Write 7-day current affairs summary
- Attempt affairscloud.com → Weekly Quiz (20 questions)
- Review 5 important legal/polity GK facts

**📝 Vocabulary:** Libel, Litigate, Locus Standi, Malfeasance, Malice, Mandate, Mediate, Mitigate, Negligence, Nominal

# 📙 PHASE 3: MOCK TESTS BEGIN (Days 151–180)
### Goal: Full-length mocks (120 questions, 2 hours). Detailed analysis. Fix weak areas.

### 🎯 MOCK TEST STRATEGY
**Where to get free mocks:**
- clat.ac.in → Official mock tests (released each year)
- LegalEdge CLAT → Free mock series
- Unacademy CLAT → Free test series
- Endeavor Careers → Free CLAT mocks
- BYJU'S CLAT → 1 free mock

**After Every Mock — 5-Step Analysis:**
1. **Score & Accuracy:** Note total score, subject-wise score, accuracy %
2. **Wrong Questions:** Write down every wrong question — WHY was it wrong? (Concept gap? Careless? Time?)
3. **Time per Section:** Did you spend too long on one section? Identify.
4. **Weak Areas:** List top 3 topics where you got most wrong. Spend next 2 days revising those.
5. **Target:** Set a score target for next mock. Improve by at least 3–5 marks per mock.

**Mock Attempt Simulation:**
- Sit in a quiet room. Phone off. Timer set for 120 minutes.
- Attempt in this order: GK (10 min) → English (25 min) → Quant (20 min) → LR (30 min) → Legal (35 min)
- Mark uncertain answers. If time allows, revisit.


---

## 📅 DAY 153 — 🧪 MOCK TEST DAY
### Full-Length Mock Test #1

**⏰ 4:00–6:00 PM | 🧪 FULL-LENGTH MOCK TEST**

**⏰ 6:00–7:00 PM | 📊 MOCK ANALYSIS (CRITICAL)**
- Step 1: Calculate raw score and subject-wise scores
- Step 2: List every wrong answer. Write the correct answer and WHY yours was wrong.
- Step 3: Identify your 3 weakest topics in this mock
- Step 4: Note time spent per section — where did you rush or slow down?
- Step 5: Set improvement target for Mock #2
- Write a 10-line "Mock Analysis Report" in your notebook

**📝 Vocabulary:** Libel, Litigate, Locus Standi, Malfeasance, Malice, Mandate, Mediate, Mitigate, Negligence, Nominal
> 📌 *Don't be disheartened by a low score. At this stage, analysis matters more than score. Every wrong answer is a lesson.*

# 📕 PHASE 4: INTENSIVE REVISION (Days 181–200)
### Goal: 2–3 mocks per week, subject-wise consolidation, eliminate weak areas.


---
## 📅 DAY 181 — 📚 SUBJECT REVISION
**⏰ 4:00–4:45 PM | ENGLISH — RC Sprint**
- Solve 3 RC passages back to back (from CLAT 2018–2024). Time: 30 minutes.
- Focus: Inference questions (most missed). Do NOT re-read passage for every question.
- **Vocabulary:** Abate, Aberrant, Abscond, Absolve, Abstain, Acrimony, Admonish, Adversity, Advocate, Affable — also REVISE last 50 words

**⏰ 4:45–5:30 PM | LEGAL REASONING — Maxims + Passage Sprint**
- Revise 20 legal maxims (write them from memory, then check)
- Solve 2 full Legal Reasoning sets. Strict 6-minute per set.

**⏰ 5:30–6:00 PM | LOGICAL REASONING**
- Solve 2 LR passage sets from CLAT 2022/2023/2024 paper
- Focus: Do NOT panic on long passages. Read conclusion sentence first.

**⏰ 6:00–6:30 PM | QUANT + GK**
- Solve 1 DI set + 5 maths MCQs. Focus on accuracy over speed.
- Read affairscloud.com → last 3 months current affairs summary
- Revise any 5 important national/international events from this year

**⏰ 6:30–7:00 PM | COMPREHENSIVE REVISION**
- Open your notebook. Revise 1 page of English notes + 1 page of Legal notes
- Say aloud: 10 legal maxims + 10 vocab words (self-testing)

---
## 🏁 EXAM WEEK STRATEGY (Last 5 Days Before CLAT 2026)

**Day Before Exam:**
- NO new study. Only light revision: 10 legal maxims, 20 vocab words, 5 GK facts.
- Sleep by 10:00 PM. Eat well. Keep admit card + ID ready.

**Exam Day Tips:**
1. Reach the center 45 minutes early.
2. Start with GK (quick marks) → English → Quant → LR → Legal.
3. Do NOT spend more than 90 seconds on any single question.
4. If stuck, mark & move. Return if time allows.
5. Never leave easy questions blank — attempt all.
6. Avoid wild guesses on uncertain answers (–0.25 per wrong).

3. **LR Notebook** — Concept notes + error log
4. **Maths Notebook** — Formulas + solved examples
5. **GK Diary** — Daily current affairs (5 facts/day)
6. **Mock Analysis Register** — Score tracker + weak area log
